                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">مَالٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Whatever one possesses:</hi> (K:) <hi rend="ital">property; wealth:</hi>] accord. to Mohammad [the Hanafee Imám), <hi rend="ital">whatever men possess, of dirhems,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">deenárs,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">gold,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">silver,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wheat,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">barley,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">bread,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">beasts,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">garments or pieces of cloth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">weapons,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">other things:</hi> (Mgh:) [<hi rend="ital">property,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wealth:</hi>] or originally <hi rend="ital">what one possesses of gold and silver:</hi> then applied to <hi rend="ital">anything that one acquires and possesses of substantial things:</hi> and mostly applied by the Arabs to <hi rend="ital">camels,</hi> because these constitute most of their wealth: (IAth, TA:) and <hi rend="ital">animals.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مَالٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Camels or sheep or goats.</hi> (S.) The <foreign lang="ar">مال</foreign> of the people of the desert consists of what are termed <foreign lang="ar">نَعَمٌ</foreign>, (T, Msb,) i. e. <hi rend="ital">Cattle, consisting of camels</hi> or <hi rend="ital">neat</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sheep</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goats,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">all these,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">camels alone;</hi> (Msb in art. <foreign lang="ar">نعم</foreign>;) <hi rend="ital">herds,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">flocks,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">herds and flocks.</hi>          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مَالٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A square in arithmetic:</hi> pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَمْوَالٌ</foreign>. See <foreign lang="ar">جَذْرٌ</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">رَجُلٌ مَالٌ</foreign>, for <foreign lang="ar">ذُومَالٍ</foreign>.
